<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="medical-practitioners-and-dentists-act-cap-253">Medical Practitioners and Dentists Act Cap (253)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#medical-practitioners-and-dentists-act-cap-253" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>In your community health nursing practice or private nurse practice you will be expected to diagnose and treat minor ailments, this encroaches on this law.</p>
<p>Narcotic Drugs and Psychotropic Substances (Control) Act 1994</p>
<p>While dealing with the dangerous drugs, you will be required to be familiar with this law.</p>
<p>This also applies to dealing with drug misuse and abuse.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="mental-health-act-cap-248">Mental Health Act Cap (248)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#mental-health-act-cap-248" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>You have been exposed to mental health and psychiatric nursing.</p>
<p>You will interact with such patients in your practice as a general nurse, midwife and community health nurse.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="other-laws-related-to-nursing-practice">Other Laws Related to Nursing Practice<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#other-laws-related-to-nursing-practice" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="medical-laboratory-technicians-and-technologists-act-1999">Medical Laboratory Technicians and Technologists Act (1999)<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#medical-laboratory-technicians-and-technologists-act-1999" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>You will be taking body specimens from patients and clients.</p>
<p>You should therefore be familiar with this law.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="clinical-medicine-act">Clinical Medicine Act<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#clinical-medicine-act" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>This law is related to the medical Practitioners and Dentists Act because of diagnosing and treating minor ailments.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="food-drugs-and-chemicals-act">Food, Drugs and Chemicals Act<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#food-drugs-and-chemicals-act" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>You will be dealing with the nutritional status of the patient. In addition, you are one of the food handlers in the hospital. Familiarise yourself with the law.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="children-and-young-persons-act">Children and Young Persons Act<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#children-and-young-persons-act" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>In your practice you will be interacting with babies, children, adolescents and teenagers. This may be in wards, departments, clinics, maternity, school health and the community. Remember children have rights which you must recognise.</p>
<p>You may be the provider of the health services, advocate or advisor of other health professionals in your multidisciplinary teams. You may have heard of the African Charter on the Rights and Welfare of the Child which was adapted by the 26th ordinary session of the Assembly of Heads of State and Government of the OAU, Addis Ababa, Ethiopia - July 1990.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="african-charter-on-the-rights-and-welfare-of-the-child">African Charter on the Rights and Welfare of the Child<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#african-charter-on-the-rights-and-welfare-of-the-child" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Any custom, tradition, cultural or religious practice that is inconsistent with the rights, duties and obligations should be discouraged.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Enjoyment of rights and freedoms is recognised and guaranteed irrespective of race, ethnic group, colour, sex, language, relation, political or other opinion, national and social origin of the child's parents or legal guardians. This includes fortune, birth or status.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Best interests of the child should be the primary consideration.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The right to life is inherent and should be protected by law. Death sentence should not be pronounced for crimes committed by the child.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Right from birth to a name. The child should be registered immediately after birth, and has a right to acquire a nationality.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Freedom of expression.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Freedom of association.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Freedom of thought, conscience and religion.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Protection of privacy.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Right to education.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Right to rest and leisure, to engage in play and recreation and cultural activities appropriate to the age of the child and to participate freely in cultural life and the arts.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>A mentally or physically disabled child has the right to special measures of protection in keeping with his physical and moral needs under conditions which ensure his dignity, promote his self reliance and active participation in the community.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Right to enjoy the best attainable state of physical, mental and spiritual health.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Protection from all forms of economic exploitation and from performing any work that is likely to be hazardous or to interfere with the child's physical, mental, spiritual, moral or social development.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Protection from all forms of torture, inhuman or degrading treatment, especially physical or mental injury or abuse, neglect or maltreatment including sexual abuse while in the care of a parent, legal guardian, or school authority or any other person who has the care of the child.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>As a nurse you are expected to:</p>
<ul>
<li>Provide necessary support for the child and for those who care for the child.</li>
<li>Identify children suffering from abuse and torture.</li>
<li>Report or refer for investigation, treatment and follow up of cases of child abuse and neglect.</li>
</ul>
<p>Get yourself a copy of the Children and Young Persons Act from the Government printers.</p>
<p>Bishops Computers
Bishops Computers</p>
<p>Workman's Compensation Act</p>
<p>You should familiarise yourself with this law. It outlines what you should do in cases of accidents during practice, with specific focus on how to go about applying for compensation of the damages caused as a result of the accident. This will assist you to advise others</p>
<p>Bill of Rights</p>
<p>In the process of the provision of health care, both the patients and the nurse have a Bill of Rights. You will study them separately.</p>
<p>The Patient's Bill of Rights</p>
<p>Earlier in the unit we discussed that health care is a right to every individual in this country. You should always remember that as you provide care to the patient, they have a right to:</p>
<ul>
<li>Considerate and respectful care.</li>
<li>Obtain complete information concerning their treatment, progress and prognosis of the disease/condition. In certain situations the patients may not be in a reasonable condition to understand or it may be medically inadvisable to give particular information. Therefore, an appropriate person should be given the information on their behalf.</li>
<li>Know by name the person caring for them.</li>
<li>Receive information necessary for them to give informed consent prior to the commencement of any procedure and/or treatment except for emergencies. The information given should include specific procedures and/or treatment, the medical risks involved, probable duration of incapacitation, where alternative significant medical care or treatment exist, or when the patient requests for information concerning medical alternatives, they have the right to such information. The patients also have the right to know the name of the person providing the treatment.</li>
<li>Refuse treatment to the extent permitted by law but must be informed of the medical consequences of their action.</li>
<li>Privacy concerning their care. Those persons not directly involved in the care must get permission from the patient in order to be present.</li>
<li>Confidentiality with regard to all communication and records pertaining to their care.</li>
<li>Expect that a hospital within its capacity can make reasonable response to the patient's request for service. The hospital must provide evaluation service and/or referral as determined by the urgency of condition. When medically permissible,</li>
</ul>
<p>patients may be transferred to another health facility only after they have received adequate information and explanation concerning the need for and alternatives to such a transfer. The receiving health institution must first have accepted the transfer for the patients.</p>
<ul>
<li>Obtain information as to any relationship of their hospital to other healthcare facilities and education institution in so far as their care is concerned.</li>
<li>Obtain information regarding the existence of any professional relationship among individuals by name who are treating them.</li>
<li>Be advised if the hospital proposes to engage in or perform human experimentation affecting their care or treatment. Patients have the right to refuse to participate in such research.</li>
<li>Expect reasonable continuity of care and have the right to know in advance appointment times and doctors availability.</li>
<li>Question and receive an explanation of their bill regardless of source of payment (Note - some medical practitioners may unnecessarily inflate the bill if the patient is insured).</li>
<li>Know what hospital rules and regulations apply to his/her conduct as a patient.</li>
</ul>
<p>Remember that all these must be followed with an overriding concern for the patient and above all the recognition of his/her dignity as a human being. Success in achieving this recognition assures success in the defence of the rights of the patient.</p>
<p>Nurses Bill of Rights</p>
<p>You as a nurse have many rights. You are entitled to human rights, and the rights of a worker.</p>
<p>As a worker you have the right to a safe environment, adequate working tools and supplies, right to risk allowance, right to professional autonomy and the right to opportunities for further education, promotion and career development.</p>
<p>Code of Regulations</p>
<p>As an employee you must acquaint yourself with the code of regulations of the organisation you have joined. If you are employed by the government of Kenya, then it is worthy to familiarise yourself with the government code of regulations which contains:</p>
<ul>
<li>Organisation of government and procedures or conduct of government business</li>
<li>The Public Service Commission</li>
</ul>
<p>Bishops Computers
Bishops Computers</p>
<ul>
<li>Correspondence; Publication and Printing</li>
<li>Terms and conditions of employment</li>
<li>Annual staff appraisal reports</li>
<li>Rules of conduct</li>
<li>Salaries, increments and seniority</li>
<li>Advances, allowances, transport, housing, medical privileges, leave, examinations and courses of training etc</li>
</ul>
<p>You are now aware that the Nursing Council of Kenya is responsible for the provision of quality care to patients and clients. This is why it is a requirement by the Council that all nurses in the country update their knowledge and skills through continuing education and professional development.</p>
<p>You are now able to differentiate between the National Nurses Association of Kenya and the Nursing Council of Kenya</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="disciplines-of-nursing-in-kenya">Disciplines of Nursing in Kenya<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#disciplines-of-nursing-in-kenya" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>You have studied the legal aspects of nursing and the Nursing Council of Kenya. You will now look at professional nursing which will start with the disciplines of nursing in Kenya.</p>
<p>The disciplines of nursing include:</p>
<ul>
<li>General Nursing</li>
<li>Midwifery</li>
<li>Community Health Nursing</li>
<li>Mental Health and Psychiatric Nursing</li>
<li>Nurse Anaesthetist</li>
<li>Ophthalmic Nursing</li>
<li>Paediatric Nursing</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="professional-nursing-practice">Professional Nursing Practice<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#professional-nursing-practice" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>You may have come across many people who think and consider nursing to be a series of practical tasks carried out by nurses and who believe that anybody can become a nurse. This interpretation does not take into account the thinking processes involved in the complex activities of assessing, planning, implementation and evaluation of the care given, nor does it acknowledge the knowledge and attitudes which must be acquired for implementing individualised nursing in various circumstances and for patients/clients from different age groups and backgrounds.</p>
<p>Despite Nightingale's early recognition of the need for a combination of intellectual and practical skills, nursing has concentrated for a very long time on the practical level rather than developing simultaneously a theoretical perspective on which to base its practice.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="clinical-practice">Clinical Practice<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#clinical-practice" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>A professional nurse in clinical practice provides clinical nursing in general nursing, midwifery and community health nursing practice. You are familiar with various definitions of nursing.</p>
<p>For the purposes of this section, the operational definition is:</p>
<p>Nursing is an art and science which aims at professional excellence in the provision of holistic care that is compassionate, culturally and socially sensitive to patients and clients.</p>
<p>Clinical nursing practice has three major roles: Provider, Advocate and Researcher.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="provider-role-in-clinical-practice">Provider Role in Clinical Practice<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#provider-role-in-clinical-practice" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>The provider role entails all those actions you will accomplish when meeting the nursing and healthcare needs of individuals, families and significant others using the nursing process. You are also expected to collaborate with other members of the nursing team and multidisciplinary teams in your practice. As you are executing the provider role you will also be playing the leadership role, which at various levels involves behavioural components such as deciding, relating, influencing and facilitating.</p>
<p>Each of these components is directed toward change, using the process of effective communication. As a leader, you will be expected to utilise interpersonal relations to effect change in the behaviour of those you relate with. You will be in leadership positions in a variety of circumstances such as assisting an individual patient or family to make change in their health related behaviours. It also involves assisting groups or communities to alter their health practices, or groups of nurses or other health professionals to effect the actions of patients or communities in achieving desirable health behaviours.</p>
<p>Another role in clinical practice is advocacy...</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="advocacy-role-in-clinical-practice">Advocacy Role in Clinical Practice<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#advocacy-role-in-clinical-practice" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>In clinical practice you are expected to play the role of a patients' advocate. This role involves: anticipating and meeting the requirements of a patient who is unable to meet their own needs. You are to be aware of the patients' needs and to communicate them to other health professionals involved in the care.</p>
<p>You will be expected to coordinate the activities of all persons involved in the provision of health care. As a provider of care and a patient's advocate you should aim at providing quality care to your patients and clients. This can be enhanced through getting involved in nursing research</p>
<p>Bishops Computers
Bishops Computers</p>
<p>Bishops Computers
Page 19 of 425
Bishops Computers</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="research-role-in-clinical-practice">Research Role in Clinical Practice<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#research-role-in-clinical-practice" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>There are various definitions of research. The core issues are emphasised in relation to generating knowledge in a systematic and scientific way. Developing nursing knowledge was initially more recognised by nurse educators than clinical practice nurses.</p>
<p>Meley (1991) in her account of the development of theoretical nursing describes how North American nurses in the 1950's recognised that without ongoing research, nursing would remain stagnant, and nursing research would not develop with the advantage of theoretical understanding. Research activities and theory development began to grow in the 1950's initially in North America but gradually spread to other parts of the world.</p>
<p>You should note that you have valuable contributions to make towards operational research at your clinical site. It is, therefore, your responsibility to make those contributions.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="characteristics-of-a-professional-nurse">Characteristics of a Professional Nurse<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#characteristics-of-a-professional-nurse" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>A professional nurse:</p>
<ul>
<li>Displays high standards of performance and integrity in nursing practice</li>
<li>Seeks constantly to improve her/his technical and interpersonal skills through continuing education and research</li>
<li>Uses sound judgement and discretion in dealing with patients/clients and their relatives</li>
<li>Provides holistic care to patients, family and community</li>
<li>Deals competently with crisis situations</li>
<li>Puts what is good for professional services to patients ahead of self-interest</li>
<li>Coordinates and evaluates nursing services in cooperation with members of other health services (collaboration and networking)</li>
<li>Is not overly concerned with the materialistic aspects of nursing</li>
<li>Expects to find satisfaction and spiritual values in their work</li>
<li>Feels responsible for the status of nursing and tries to advance and never to retard it</li>
<li>Has inner resources to which she/he can turn to, for renewal of faith and courage when weary and discouraged</li>
<li>Is proud of her/his profession and considers it to be at par with other professions like medicine or law or any other vocation practised for compensation, which at the same time contributes in its own unique way to the welfare of humanity</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="how-can-you-make-those-contributions">How can you make those contributions?<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#how-can-you-make-those-contributions" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>You must constantly be on the alert of nursing problems and important questions about your nursing practice. This can serve as the basis of articulating research problem areas. Since you are directly involved in providing care, you are often in the best position to identify such questions and problems.</p>
<p>You have a responsibility to become actively involved in research studies.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="how-can-you-be-involved-in-research">How can you be involved in research?<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#how-can-you-be-involved-in-research" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>You are already in one way or another involved in research through the massive data you collect from day to day. Your shortcoming is that you do not know how to utilise the data. In this course you will learn about data collection and interpretation of the data to other health care professionals or to patients and their families. The details will be covered in module four.</p>
<p>What you need to remember now is that you must be continually aware of studies that are directly related to your areas of clinical practice. You must share the findings with your colleagues and utilise them in an attempt to improve patients' care.</p>
<p>Remember, when research studies are not made available to other nurses, the impact of the findings on nursing practice is diminished. You should be aware that the future of nursing science depends on active involvement of nurses in the implementation and utilisation of nursing research.</p>
<p>Nurses must develop curiosity about nursing practice. Their belief in the worth of nursing practice is emphasised by the acceptance of the research role and responsibility.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="nursing-education">Nursing Education<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-education" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>There are several aspects of nursing education. In Kenya there are nursing programmes regulated by the Nursing Council of Kenya and continuing nursing education conducted at areas of practice. We will start by looking at the basic programmes.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="basic-programmes">Basic Programmes<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#basic-programmes" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>There are three levels of nursing programmes.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="degree-programmes">Degree Programmes<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#degree-programmes" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>The five universities offering bachelor in nursing for school leavers are:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>University of Eastern Africa, Baraton which started in 1988</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>University of Nairobi which started in March 1992</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Moi University which started in September 1998</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>KENYATTA University</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Kenya Methodist University (KRCHN - BScN upgrading)</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Other programmes offering first degrees in nursing for registered nurses are conducted at KMTC Nairobi in collaboration with the University of Dundee, Scotland; the Aga Khan University Kenya Campus and the American World University.</p>
<p>Egerton University, Tropical Institute of Community Health in Kisumu has also shown an interest in offering such courses.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="diploma-programmes">Diploma Programmes<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#diploma-programmes" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>There are two basic programmes in Kenya: the Kenya Registered Nursing (KRN) and Kenya Registered Community Health Nursing (KRCHN).</p>
<p>KRN is being conducted at the Nairobi Hospital and Mater hospital in Nairobi. KRCHN is being conducted by many schools of nursing sponsored by the government, mission and private organisations.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="certificate-programmes">Certificate Programmes<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#certificate-programmes" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>The only certificate nursing programme that is currently in place is the Kenya Enrolled Community Health Nursing which is being conducted by the government, mission and private institutions.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="basic-programmes">Basic Programmes<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#basic-programmes" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>All these programmes are tailored in such a way that there is an integration of general nursing, midwifery, community health nursing, mental health and psychiatric nursing.</p>
<p>Apart from the basic programmes there are post-basic programmes at diploma and certificate levels covering midwifery, community health nursing and mental health and psychiatric nursing, nurse anaesthetist, ophthalmic nursing and paediatric nursing.</p>
<p>Institutions offering higher education at master's level for nurses are:</p>
<ul>
<li>University of Nairobi offering Masters in Nursing</li>
<li>Kenyatta University offering Masters in Public Health and Epidemiology</li>
<li>KMTC offering Masters in Medical Education and Masters in Nursing in collaboration with University of Dundee</li>
</ul>
<p>Other places which also admit nurses for a master's degree are Moi University and University of Nairobi. All the tutors or lecturers teaching in these programmes are practising in nursing education.</p>
<p>The Nursing Council of Kenya is advocating that all nurses update their knowledge and skills through continuing education conducted in workshops, seminars and case presentations or on the job training. The main aim is the provision of quality care to patients and to keep abreast with scientific and technological developments.</p>
<p>You read earlier that nursing research can be conducted in the clinical area. You can now add to that. that research is also conducted in nursing education to improve its quality.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="section-2-the-nursing-process">SECTION 2: THE NURSING PROCESS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#section-2-the-nursing-process" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="introduction">Introduction<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#introduction" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>This second section will introduce you to professionalism and the nursing process. It will build on what you have already learnt and it will also serve as revision.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="objectives">Objectives<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#objectives" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>By the end of this section you will be able to:</p>
<ul>
<li>Define the nursing process</li>
<li>Describe the rationale of using the nursing process</li>
<li>List the steps of the nursing process</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="definition-of-the-nursing-process">Definition of the Nursing Process<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#definition-of-the-nursing-process" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>The nursing process is a technique which scientifically attempts to solve problems created by the patient's illness and to meet the health care and nursing needs of patients.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="rationale-for-using-the-nursing-process">Rationale for Using the Nursing Process<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#rationale-for-using-the-nursing-process" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<p>The nursing process introduces a concept of objective measurement into nursing management at the bed side. It compels you as the nurse to look more closely at the problems as the patient sees them rather than as you assume the problems to be. Furthermore, it defines what the nursing role is all about and creates a boundary within which you can safely practise clinical skills.</p>
<p>The nursing process establishes nurse-patient relationship on a firm basis because it is objective and is a total care technique. The care plan, being related to one individual, gives you as a nurse greater professional job satisfaction. The nursing process, apart from being practical, is also a research tool since you can collect data that is retrospective, current and prospective.</p>
<p>Bishops Computers
Bishops Computers</p>
<p>With regards to patients problems, how do you define a problem?</p>
<p>A problem is any condition or situation which requires nursing intervention for the patient to regain a state of health or towards a peaceful death.</p>
<p>In learning the art of applying the nursing process, you are applying science which is the skilled art of making the well and the sick more comfortable and to feel well cared for.</p>
<p>You may have already used the nursing process. As a reminder, however, the steps are:</p>
<ol>
<li>Assessment</li>
<li>Planning</li>
<li>Implementation</li>
<li>Evaluation</li>
</ol>
<p>Assessment</p>
<p>Assessment starts with your very first encounter with the patient. It involves a systematic collection of data conducted on a patient, done to determine their health status and to identify any actual or potential health problems in order to formulate a nursing diagnosis, this becomes the basis of the nursing care plan. A sensitive and continuous nursing assessment by means of nursing history and health assessment is essential in maintaining awareness of the nursing care that a patient receives.</p>
<p>The nursing history is taken for the purposes of determining the patient's state of illness. It also provides you as a nurse with the opportunity to collect the data and to convey interest, support and understanding to the patient.</p>
<p>The skill used in obtaining history is interviewing. An interview is a dialogue between patients and you as their nurse, which is a very personal experience.</p>
<p>Interviewing is a process that requires wisdom, judgement, tact and experience. It involves a sensitive direction of a conversation with patients in order to obtain information about them.</p>
<p>Your approach to the patient will largely determine the amount and quality of information that you will receive.</p>
<p>Achieving a relationship of mutual trust and respect will require the ability to communicate a sincere interest in the patient.</p>
<p>You must make the patient as comfortable as possible and offer privacy for the interview.</p>
<p>The skills involved in interviewing a patient include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Listening and questioning</li>
<li>Observing and interpreting</li>
<li>Synthesising</li>
<li>Incorporating what is learnt into a plan of care</li>
</ul>
<p>The Process of Interviewing</p>
<p>The process of interviewing involves:</p>
<ul>
<li>Talking and listening to the patient</li>
<li>Allowing the patient to tell their story in their own way</li>
<li>Looking for the main area of concern</li>
<li>Giving the patient time, without interruption, to tell you why they are seeking help</li>
<li>Being attentive not only to the patient's verbal expression but also to their non-verbal behaviour which may be displayed in the form of gestures, postures and facial expressions</li>
<li>Anticipating the patients' anxieties and trying to relieve them</li>
<li>Making relevant enquiries</li>
<li>Ensuring that the client feels that they are being understood</li>
</ul>
<p>The Process of Interviewing</p>
<p>Health facilities have developed their own interview guides but what is important is to conduct a thorough assessment of the patient with regard to their basic human needs and their state of wellness or illness.</p>
<p>A variety of models can serve as the framework for the assessment of basic needs. These include Functional Health Patterns (Gordon:1982), Maslow's Hierarchy of Needs and Eriksson's Eight Stages of Human Development.</p>
<p>Assessment of the total needs of the patient includes their physical, psychological, emotional, intellectual, developmental, social, cultural and spiritual needs.</p>
<p>Health Assessment</p>
<p>How would you conduct a health assessment?</p>
<p>The health assessment of the patient may be carried out prior to, during or following the nursing history, depending on the patient's physical and emotional state, their response to their illness and hospitalisation, and the immediate priorities of their illness situation.</p>
<p>What is the purpose of health assessment?</p>
<p>The purpose of the health assessment is to identify the parameters of physical, psychological and emotional function that include a nursing need that exists. The</p>
<p>Bishops Computers
Bishops Computers</p>
<p>techniques and skills that are utilised in conducting the health assessment include:</p>
<ul>
<li>Use of the senses of sight, touch, hearing and smell</li>
<li>Use of appropriate interview skills and techniques</li>
<li>Physical examination</li>
<li>Techniques and strategies for assessing behaviours and role changes</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="the-physical-examination">The Physical Examination<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#the-physical-examination" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>You have been performing physical examinations on patients in various situations.</p>
<p>A physical examination is designed to determine the patient's assets which may serve to compensate for their limitations. Therefore, to accomplish the purposes of the physical examination, you must be skilled in the techniques of inspection, palpation, percussion and auscultation.</p>
<p>You must also have a sound basic knowledge of anatomy and physiology and of the symptomatology of the disease process with which the patient presents.</p>
<p>You must learn to observe with the 'seeing' eyes, hear with the 'hearing' ears, feel with 'feeling' hands and interpret the findings of the examination.</p>
<p>At the completion of the nursing history and health assessment, you should inform the patient how the data will be used, the conclusions that will be drawn, and the fact that they and their family or significant others will be involved in developing the plan for care. By the termination of the assessment they should know who you are as their nurse and how they can communicate with you.</p>
<p>You are familiar with performing a physical examination which is usually carried out following the health history. In order to facilitate the data collection process, the assessment is performed in well lit, warm area. The patient is undressed and draped appropriately so that only the area to be examined is exposed.</p>
<p>The physical and psychological comfort of the patient is considered at all times. If a particular manoeuvre may cause discomfort, an explanation of what to expect precedes that part of examination. Fingernails are kept short to avoid injuring the patient. The examination is to be performed in an organised and systematic manner. This encourages cooperation and trust on the part of the patient.</p>
<p>The patient's health history provides you with a complete health profile that guides all aspects of the physical assessment. In addition, it helps you to focus on body organs and systems that are of particular concern to the patient.</p>
<p>The basic tools of the physical examination are the human senses of vision, hearing, touch and smell. These human tools may be augmented by special man-made appliances, for example, stethoscope and ophthalmoscope.</p>
<p>The first fundamental process in physical examination is inspection, and the power to observe must be cultivated.</p>
<p>A general inspection is carried out at the first contact with the patient.</p>
<p>While creating rapport by introducing yourself to the patient, shaking their hand and talking to them, many impressions register in this exchange, and numerous valuable observations can be made.</p>
<p>For example, age can be assessed, the general appearance whether thin or fat, anxious or depressed, body structure normal or deformed, posture and stature, body movements, nutritional status, speech pattern and body temperature. The physical examination requires a systematic approach of a head to toe and is accompanied by:</p>
<ul>
<li>Taking vital signs such as temperature, pulse, respiration and blood pressure</li>
<li>Measuring height, weight, fluid intake and output</li>
<li>Auscultating for body sounds of the lungs, the navel and other organs using stethoscope</li>
<li>Palpating soft areas of the body to check for solid masses, abnormal rigidity or tenderness</li>
</ul>
<p>You will review physical examination again when you study the clinical diagnosis.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="nursing-diagnosis">Nursing Diagnosis<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-diagnosis" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>After the completion of the nursing history and the health assessment, you should analyse, synthesise and summarise the data collected and determine the patient's need for nursing care. You should also identify the actual or potential health problems responsive to resolution by nursing actions as nursing diagnosis.</p>
<p>When developing the nursing diagnosis for a particular patient, you must first identify the commonalities among the assessment data you have collected. These common features lead to the categorisation of related data that reveals the problem that needs nursing intervention. Therefore, the patient's nursing problem is defined as the nursing diagnosis.</p>
<p>Remember that nursing diagnosis is not medical diagnosis or medical treatment or diagnostic studies. Nursing diagnoses are the patient's actual or potential problems that are</p>
<p>Bishops Computers
Bishops Computers</p>
<p>enumerable to resolution by nursing actions. Nursing diagnoses that are succinctly stated in terms of the specific problems of the patient will guide you to develop a nursing care plan.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="recording-the-nursing-diagnosis">Recording the Nursing Diagnosis<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#recording-the-nursing-diagnosis" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>You should record the patient's nursing diagnosis in the nursing care plan as well as in the patient problem list.</p>
<p>A problem is defined as anything that concerns the patient, endangers their health, requires management and concerns any member of the health care team.</p>
<p>You have already gone through the assessment steps of the nursing process by looking at the data collection methods, that is, interview, observation, physical examination and taking vital observations.</p>
<p>Remember you will be required to utilise communication, interpersonal and client-provider skills in conducting the assessment, collecting and analysing data using subjective and making objective observations and performing the necessary physical examination. This is followed by formulating a nursing or medical diagnosis to clarify client's needs.</p>
<p>Then comes arranging the client's needs accordingly in order of priority, and forming partnership with clients in assessing their care needs and determining appropriate intervention strategies to address them.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="planning">Planning<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#planning" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Once you identify the nursing diagnosis, the next step is to develop the planning components of the nursing process. This phase involves:</p>
<ul>
<li>Setting priorities to the nursing diagnoses specifying immediate, intermediate and long term goals of nursing action</li>
<li>Identifying specific nursing interventions, appropriate for attaining goals.</li>
<li>Identifying interdependent interventions</li>
<li>Documenting the nursing diagnosis, goals, nursing interventions and expected outcomes on the nursing care plan</li>
</ul>
<p>During this phase of the nursing process, it is your responsibility to communicate with the appropriate persons any assessment data indicative of health needs that can be met by other members of the health care team.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="setting-priorities">Setting Priorities<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#setting-priorities" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Setting priorities for the nursing diagnoses should be a process of collaboration between you and the patient or their family members.</p>
<p>Consideration must be given to the urgency of the problem, with the most crucial problems receiving the highest priority.</p>
<p>Maslow's hierarchy of needs provides a useful framework for the determination of priority problems. The use of this hierarchy requires that high priorities be given to physical needs. After the priorities of the physical needs are met, subsequent priorities are reassigned according to the urgency of needs at other levels of the hierarchy.</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20260110-4f1ff7a1.jpeg" alt="img-3.jpeg"></p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="establishing-goals-for-nursing-action">Establishing Goals for Nursing Action<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#establishing-goals-for-nursing-action" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>After establishing the priorities of the nursing diagnosis, identify the immediate, intermediate and long-term goals and the nursing actions appropriate for the attainment of your goals. You should include the patients and the family in the establishment of the goals for the nursing actions.</p>
<ul>
<li>Immediate Goals: Immediate goals address existing problems.</li>
<li>Intermediate Goals: Intermediate goals address the potential problems likely to occur in the near future.</li>
<li>Long Term Goals: Long term goals require longer periods of time for their accomplishment. This usually involves prevention of complications and further health problems, health education and rehabilitation.</li>
</ul>
<p>You should involve the patient and the family in decision-making about the nursing interventions to meet the goals. Involvement of the patient and the family in the planning of nursing interventions promotes their cooperation in the implementation of the nursing care.</p>
<p>Bishops Computers
Bishops Computers</p>
<p>The identification of appropriate nursing interventions and their related goals depends on your recognition of the strengths and potential of the patient and the family; his understanding of the patho-physiological alterations that he experiences and his sensitivity to his emotional, psychological and intellectual response to his state of illness.</p>
<p>In addition, your knowledge of nursing, your clinical experience and awareness of available supporting resources influence the validity of the nursing interventions that you identify as appropriate in resolving the patient's nursing diagnosis.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="establishing-expected-outcomes">Establishing Expected Outcomes<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#establishing-expected-outcomes" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>You should state the expected outcomes of the nursing interactions.</p>
<p>These outcomes should be stated in terms of the patient's behaviour. They should be realistic and measurable.</p>
<p>What you should realise is that:</p>
<ul>
<li>The outcomes that define the expected behaviour of the patient will serve as the basis for evaluation of the effectiveness of the nursing interventions.</li>
<li>The critical time periods provide a time frame for determining effectiveness of the nursing interventions and existence of a need for additional or altered nursing care.</li>
</ul>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="formulating-the-nursing-care-plan">Formulating the Nursing Care Plan<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#formulating-the-nursing-care-plan" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>The nursing care plan serves to communicate the following information to all members of the nursing team:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>The nursing diagnosis and priorities</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The goals of the nursing intervention</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The nursing interventions which are expressed in the form of nursing orders</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The expected outcomes which identify the expected behavioural responses of the patient</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>The critical time periods within which each outcome must be met</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20260110-4624fb10.jpeg" alt="img-4.jpeg"></p>
<p>You must write down the precise behaviour expected in the nursing care plan. It should be written in a systematic manner that facilitates its use by all nursing personnel. You should provide space in the care plan for the documentation of the patient's response in the nursing interventions and the outcomes.</p>
<p>The nursing care plan is subject to change as the patients problems change or as the priorities of the problem and resolution of the problems shift and as additional information about the patient's state of health is collected.</p>
<p>As you implement nursing interventions, the patient's responses are evaluated and documented and the care plan changed accordingly. A well-developed and continuously updated nursing care plan is the greatest assistance to the patient, since their nursing diagnosis will be resolved and their needs will be met.</p>
<p>Bishops Computers
Bishops Computers</p>

<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="implementation">Implementation<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#implementation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Implementation of the nursing process follows the formulation of the nursing care plan. Implementation refers to carrying out the proposed plan of care. You should assume responsibility for the nursing team, or other members of the health care team as appropriate. You are to coordinate the activities of all persons involved in the implementation.</p>
<p>Keep in mind that:</p>
<ul>
<li>The nursing care plan serves as the basis for implementation.</li>
<li>The immediate, intermediate and long-term goals are used as a focus for the implementation of the designed nursing interventions.</li>
<li>While implementing nursing care, you are to continually assess the patient and their response to the nursing care.</li>
<li>Alterations are made in the care plan as the patient's condition, problems, and responses change, and priorities are thus reassigned.</li>
</ul>
<p>Implementation includes all of the nursing interventions that are directed toward resolution of the patient's diagnosis and meeting their health needs.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="nursing-interventions-include">Nursing interventions include:<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#nursing-interventions-include" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Hygienic care</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Promotion of physical and psychological comfort</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Support of respiratory and elimination functions</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Facilitation of the ingestion of food, fluids and nutrients</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Environmental management health teaching</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Promotion of a therapeutic relationship</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>You should use judgement and decision-making skills in the selection of nursing interventions that are based on physiological principles. You will also need to integrate and apply your knowledge of physiology. All nursing interventions are patient-focused and goal directed. They are based on scientific principles. You should implement them with compassion, confidence and willingness to understand the patient's problems.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="delegating-nursing-action">Delegating Nursing Action<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#delegating-nursing-action" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>You may delegate certain specific actions to other members of the nursing team. When delegating, you must:</p>
<ul>
<li>Know the capabilities and limitations of the members of the nursing team.</li>
<li>Select the most appropriate person to implement and supervise the performance of the actions.</li>
<li>You should provide the nursing team members with all information that is needed to perform the actions in such a way that the patient remains at all times the focus of the actions.</li>
<li>You should communicate verbally and in writing to the appropriate persons the coordination and continuity of care, information about the patient's responses to their care and any changes that must be made in the plan of care. This is because</li>
</ul>
<p>Bishops Computers
Page 25 of 425
Bishops Computers</p>
<p>many members of the nursing team and health care team are involved in the patient's care. Continuous updating of the care plan is of paramount importance in ensuring coordination and continuity of care.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="recording-outcomes">Recording Outcomes<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#recording-outcomes" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>The implementation phase of the nursing process is concluded when the nursing interventions have been completed and the patient's responses to them have been recorded. You should concisely and objectively make the recordings.</p>
<p>The recordings should:</p>
<ul>
<li>Relate to the nursing diagnosis</li>
<li>Describe the nursing interventions and the patient's response to the interventions</li>
<li>Include any additional pertinent data</li>
</ul>
<p>You can make good evaluation after accurate recording. Documentation of information therefore provides the basis for the measurement of the patient's behavioural response to the nursing intervention.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="evaluation">Evaluation<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#evaluation" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Evaluation is the final component to the nursing process. It is directed towards determining the patient's response to the nursing intervention and the extent to which the goals have been achieved.</p>
<p>The nursing care plan, therefore, provides the basis for evaluating the nursing diagnosis, goals, and nursing interventions. Expected outcomes provide the specific guidelines that dictate the focus of evaluation.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="what-is-the-rationale-for-using-the-nursing-process">What is the rationale for using the Nursing Process<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#what-is-the-rationale-for-using-the-nursing-process" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h3 level="3" id="did-you-think-of-the-following">Did you think of the following?<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#did-you-think-of-the-following" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h3></div>
<ul>
<li>Introduces a concept of objective measurement into nursing management at the bed side.</li>
<li>Compels the nurse to look more closely at the problems as the patient sees them, rather than assuming them.</li>
<li>Defines what the nursing role is all about and creates a boundary within which to safely practice clinical skills.</li>
<li>Establishes nurse patient relationship on a firm basis because it is objective and is a total technique.</li>
<li>Is a research tool for collecting retrospective, current and prospective data</li>
</ul>

        // Theme toggle functionality
        const themeToggle = document.getElementById('theme-toggle');
        const html = document.documentElement;
        
        themeToggle.addEventListener('click', () => {
            const currentTheme = html.getAttribute('data-theme');
            const newTheme = currentTheme === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light';
            
            html.setAttribute('data-theme', newTheme);
            localStorage.setItem('theme', newTheme);
        });
        
        // Load saved theme
        const savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('theme') || 'light';
        html.setAttribute('data-theme', savedTheme);
